#################################
#################################
### missile scripted triggers ###
#################################
#################################


sea_launch_point_ = {
	always = no
}

sea_launch_point_0 = {
	always = no
}

### launch point triggers ###

#Grønland
sea_launch_point_1 = {
	meta_trigger = {
		text = {
			THIS = {
		OR = {
			#Labrador Sea
			ships_in_area = {
				area = 50
				size > [ship_number_LAM]
				type = artillery
			}
			#Denmark Strait
			ships_in_area = {
				area = 44
				size > [ship_number_LAM]
				type = artillery
			}
			# 
		}
			}
		}
		ship_number_LAM = "[?THIS.var_ship_number_LAM]"
	}
}

				type = anti_tank
				type = submarine
			}
			# 
			# 
		
			}
		}
		sub_number_LAM = "[?THIS.var_sub_number_LAM]"
	}
}

	always = no
}

	always = no
}
